Let's start by checking the path from V12 to V18. The path is:

P(V12) = P(V12 | V9) \* P(V9) + P(V12 | not V9) \* P(not V9)

P(V12 | V9) = P(V12, V9) / P(V9) = (1/2) / (1/2) = 1

P(V12 | not V9) = P(V12, not V9) / P(not V9) = (1/2) / (1/2) = 1

P(V9) = P(V12 | V9) \* P(V9) + P(V12 | not V9) \* P(not V9) = 1 + 1 = 2
